<script>
window.addEventListener("message", function (event) {
    const data = event.data;

    if (!data || !data.frameHeight || !data.frameSrc) return;

    // Select all iframes with the class "autoResizeFrame"
    const frames = document.querySelectorAll(".autoResizeFrame");

    frames.forEach(function (frame) {
        // Clean URLs to avoid mismatch due to params
        const frameUrl = frame.src.split("#")[0].split("?")[0];
        const postedUrl = data.frameSrc.split("#")[0].split("?")[0];

        if (frameUrl === postedUrl) {
            frame.style.height = data.frameHeight + "px";
        }
    });
});
</script>
<!-- common script for embed iframes -->

<script>
document.querySelector('#clickSearchValue').onclick = function(){
	if(document.getElementById("searchText2").value != 'Type Your search'){
	   let a = document.getElementById("searchText2").value;
       a = a.replace(/(^\s+|[^a-zA-Z0-9\u0900-\u097F ]+|\s+$)/g,"-");  
	   a = a.replace(/\s+/g,"-");
	   window.location.href="/search?q="+a.toLowerCase();
       return false
	   
	}
}

document.getElementById("clickSearchValue").disabled = true;
document.getElementById("searchText2").onkeyup = function() {
	if(document.getElementById("searchText2").value !=""){
	  document.getElementById("clickSearchValue").disabled = false;
	}	 
};
</script><!--End of megaMenu-->

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-button');
        const contents = document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content');

        buttons.forEach(button => {
            button.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const tabId = button.getAttribute('data-tab');

                buttons.forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
                contents.forEach(content => content.classList.remove('active'));

                button.classList.add('active');
                document.getElementById(tabId).classList.add('active');
            });
        });
    });
</script>

<script>
    const searchBox = document.getElementById("locationSearch");
    const searchResults = document.getElementById("searchResults");

    const aqiCategories = [
        { min: 0, max: 50, category: "Good" },
        { min: 51, max: 100, category: "Moderate" },
        { min: 101, max: 150, category: "Poor" },
        { min: 151, max: 200, category: "Unhealthy" },
        { min: 201, max: 300, category: "Severe" },
        { min: 301, max: 500, category: "Hazardous" },
    ];

    function getAQICategory(aqi) {
        const category = aqiCategories.find(range => aqi >= range.min && aqi <= range.max);
        return category ? category.category : "N/A";
    }
	
	function getAQIRange(aqi) {
		const category = aqiCategories.find(range => aqi >= range.min && aqi <= range.max);
		return category
			? { category: category.category, range: `${category.min}-${category.max}` }
			: { category: "N/A", range: "N/A" };
	}
	
	  // ===============================
    // CITY SLUG GENERATOR
    // ===============================
    function generateCitySlug(cityName) {
        return cityName
            .toLowerCase()
            .trim()
            .replace(/\s+/g, "-")
            .replace(/[^a-z\-]/g, "") + "-air-quality-index-today";
    }

    searchBox.addEventListener("input", () => {
        const query = searchBox.value.toLowerCase().trim();

        searchResults.innerHTML = "";
        searchResults.style.display = "none";

        if (!query) return;

        const filteredData = jsonData.filter(item =>
            item.city_name.toLowerCase().includes(query)
        );
        // console.log("==filteredData==");
        // console.log(filteredData);

        if (filteredData.length > 0) {
            searchResults.style.display = "block";
            filteredData.forEach(item => {
                const div = document.createElement("div");
                div.className = "result-item";
                div.textContent = `${item.city_name}, ${item.state_name}`;
               /* div.addEventListener("click", () => {
                    searchBox.value = `${item.city_name}, ${item.state_name}`;
                    updateAQIData(item); 
                    updateFAQ(item);
                });*/
				/*div.addEventListener("click", () => {
					// Save selected city to LocalStorage
					localStorage.setItem("selectedAQICity", item.city_name);
					// Redirect to AQI page
					window.location.href = "/aqi";
				});*/
				div.addEventListener("click", () => {
                const slug = generateCitySlug(item.city_name);
               // const url = `https://beta.tv9hindi.com/aqi/${slug}`;
				const url = `/aqi/${slug}`;
                window.location.href = url;
            });
                searchResults.appendChild(div);
            });
        }
    });

    function updateAQIData(data) 
	{
        // console.log(data);
		const safeValue = (value, placeholder = "-") =>
            value !== undefined && value !== null && value !== "" ? value : placeholder;
		
		/*const date = new Date(data.last_updatedat);
		
		const optionsDate = { day: "2-digit", month: "long", year: "numeric" };
		const optionsTime = { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit", hour12: true };
		
		const formattedDate = date.toLocaleDateString("en-GB", optionsDate); // 11 December 2024
		const formattedTime = date.toLocaleTimeString("en-GB", optionsTime); // 8:29 AM
		
		const formattedDateTime = `${formattedDate} | ${formattedTime}`;
		*/
		
		const { category, range } = getAQIRange(data.aqi);
        document.getElementById("cityName").textContent = safeValue(data.city_name, "N/A");
        document.getElementById("aqiValue").textContent = safeValue(data.aqi, "N/A");
        document.getElementById("aqiCategory").textContent = safeValue(category, "N/A");
        document.getElementById("pm25Value").textContent = safeValue(data.pm25, "N/A");
        document.getElementById("pm10Value").textContent = safeValue(data.pm10, "N/A");
        document.getElementById("aqiRange").textContent = `range: ${safeValue(range, "N/A")}`;
        //document.getElementById("lastUpdated").textContent = `Last Updated: ${safeValue(formattedDateTime, "N/A")}`;

        // console.log("oocnnn++"+data.city_name);
		const wrapperElement = document.getElementById("AQIContent_Wrapper");
		const newClass = `${category.toLowerCase()}AQI`;
		wrapperElement.className = `AQIContent_Wrapper ${newClass}`;
		
		searchResults.style.display = "none";
    }

	function getCityData(cityName) {
	  return jsonData.find(city => city.city_name.toLowerCase() === cityName.toLowerCase());
	}
	

	document.querySelectorAll("figure[data-city]").forEach(figure => {
	  figure.addEventListener("click", event => {
		event.preventDefault();
	
		const cityName = figure.getAttribute("data-city");
		const cityData = getCityData(cityName);

        // console.log("cityName=="+cityName);
        // console.log("cityData==");
        // console.log(cityData);

		if (cityData) {
		  updateAQIData(cityData);
        
		} else {
		  console.error(`No AQI data available for city: ${cityName}`);
		}
	  });
	});






</script>

<script>
function initScrollHandler(){
  let scrollTimer;
  const body = document.body;
  document.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
    if (scrollTimer) return;
    scrollTimer = requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      const scrollTop = window.scrollY;
      if (scrollTop >= 22) {
        body.classList.add('sticky');
      } else {
        body.classList.remove('sticky');
      }
      scrollTimer = null;
    });
  }, {passive: true});
}
if(document.readyState==='loading'){
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',initScrollHandler);
}else{
  initScrollHandler();
}
</script>
<script>
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    if (window.innerWidth > 768) return; 
    let lastScroll = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
    const body = document.body;
    window.addEventListener("scroll", function () {
      const currentScroll = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
      if (currentScroll <= 2) {
        body.classList.remove("scrollT", "scrollB");
      } else if (currentScroll > lastScroll) {
        body.classList.remove("scrollT");
        body.classList.add("scrollB");
      } else if (currentScroll < lastScroll) {
        body.classList.remove("scrollB");
        body.classList.add("scrollT");
      }
      lastScroll = currentScroll;
    });
  });
</script>
<script>
function initStickyHandler(){
  let scrollPos = 0;
  let stickyTimer;
  const body = document.body;
  window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
    if (stickyTimer) return;
    stickyTimer = requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      const currentPos = body.getBoundingClientRect().top;
      if (currentPos > scrollPos) {
        body.classList.add("sticky-up");
        body.classList.remove("sticky-down");                
      } else {
        body.classList.remove("sticky-up");
        body.classList.add("sticky-down");
      }
      scrollPos = currentPos;
      stickyTimer = null;
    });
  }, {passive: true});
}
if(document.readyState==='loading'){
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',initStickyHandler);
}else{
  initStickyHandler();
}
</script>

<script>

// Lazy Load Images using Intersection Observer
(function () 
{
	var observer = new IntersectionObserver(onIntersect);
	document.querySelectorAll(".lazy").forEach((img) => 
	{
		observer.observe(img);
	});
	document.querySelectorAll(".lozad").forEach((img) => 
	{
		observer.observe(img);
	});
	document.querySelectorAll("[data-lazy]").forEach((img) => 
	{
		observer.observe(img);
	});
	
  document.querySelectorAll('[loading="lazy"]').forEach((img) => 
	{
		observer.observe(img);
	});
  
	/*
	document.querySelectorAll('.wp-post-image').forEach((img) => 
	{
		observer.observe(img);
	});
	
	document.querySelectorAll('[data-src*="image"]').forEach((img) => 
	{
		observer.observe(img);
	});
  */
	

  document.querySelectorAll("[data-video]").forEach((entrys) => 
	{
    if (entrys.getAttribute("data-video") == false) {
      entrys.setAttribute("src", entrys.getAttribute("data-src"));
      entrys.setAttribute("data-video", true);
    }
    observer.observe(entrys);
  });
  
	function onIntersect(entries) 
	{
		entries.forEach((entry) => 
		{
			if (entry.target.getAttribute("data-processed") || !entry.isIntersecting)
				return true;
        if(entry.target.getAttribute("data-src") != undefined || entry.target.getAttribute("data-src") != null){
          entry.target.setAttribute("src", entry.target.getAttribute("data-src"));
          entry.target.setAttribute("data-processed", true);
        }
		});
	}
})();

  if('IntersectionObserver' in window){
    const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
      entries.forEach(entry => {
        if(entry.isIntersecting && !entry.target.dataset.loaded){
          const img = entry.target;
          const src = img.dataset.src;
          if(src){
            img.src = src;
            img.dataset.loaded = 'true';
            observer.unobserve(img);
          }
        }
      });
    }, {rootMargin: '50px'});
    
    document.querySelectorAll('.lazy, .lozad, [data-src]').forEach(img => observer.observe(img));
  }
}

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',initLazyLoad);
}else{
  setTimeout(initLazyLoad,0);
}*/

<script type="text/javascript">
function initGA4Events(){
  const dl = window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
  
  document.querySelectorAll('.language_menu .container').forEach(item => {
    item.addEventListener('click', function(){
      dl.push({event:'language_selection',site_language:this.innerText});
    }, {passive:true});
  });
  
  document.querySelectorAll('.catHead').forEach(item => {
    item.addEventListener('click', function(){
      dl.push({event:'hamburger_menu_click',main_menu_name:this.innerText,sub_menu_name:'NA'});
    }, {passive:true});
  });
  
  document.querySelectorAll('.subItems li a').forEach(item => {
    item.addEventListener('click', function(){
      const mainMenu = this.closest('.hassubmenu')?.querySelector('.catHead')?.innerText || 'NA';
      dl.push({event:'hamburger_menu_click',main_menu_name:mainMenu,sub_menu_name:this.innerText});
    }, {passive:true});
  });
  
  document.querySelectorAll('.view_more').forEach(item => {
    item.addEventListener('click', function(){
      const widget = this.parentElement.querySelector('.tv9common-heading h2, .heading h2')?.innerText;
      if(widget) dl.push({event:'view_more_click',click_name:this.innerText,widget_name:widget});
    }, {passive:true});
  });
}

if(document.readyState === 'loading'){
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initGA4Events);
} else {
  initGA4Events();
}
</script>


<script type="text/javascript">
function initExtraGA4Events(){
  const dl = window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];

  // news_subcategory_cta
  document.querySelectorAll('.stateMenu').forEach((item, index) => {
    item.addEventListener('click', function(){
      dl.push({
        event: 'news_subcategory_cta',
        widget_name: 'Home Page State',
        click_name: this.innerText.trim(),
        click_position: index + 1 // pass correct position of CTA
      });
    }, {passive:true});
  });

  // Widget Tracking - common-heading
  document.querySelectorAll('.tv9common-heading').forEach((item, index) => {
    const heading = item.querySelector('h2');
    if(heading){
      item.addEventListener('click', function(){
        dl.push({
          event: 'widgets_tracking',
          widget_name: heading.innerText.trim(),
          click_position: index + 1
        });
      }, {passive:true});
    }
  });

  // Widget Tracking - Weather
  document.querySelectorAll('.weather_icon').forEach((item, index) => {
    item.addEventListener('click', function () {
      dl.push({
        event: 'widgets_tracking',
        widget_name: 'weather_forecast',
        click_position: index + 1
      });
    }, { passive: true });
  });

  
   // Widget Tracking - Google Preferred Source Badge
  document.querySelectorAll('.google_badge_icon a, .googlePrefStickyMob a').forEach((item, index) => {
    item.addEventListener('click', function () {
      dl.push({
        event: 'widgets_tracking',
        widget_name: 'google_preferred_source',
        click_position: index + 1
      });
    }, { passive: true });
  });


  
}

if(document.readyState === 'loading'){
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initExtraGA4Events);
} else {
  initExtraGA4Events();
}
</script>

<script>
function initVideoTracking(){
  window.addEventListener("message", (e) => {
    if(e.origin === "https://static.vidgyor.com") {
      const iframe = document.getElementById("vidgyor_iframe");
      if(iframe && e.data.msg){
        (window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || []).push({
          'event':`live_tv_${e.data.msg}`,
          'video_url': iframe.src
        });
      }
    }
  }, {passive:true});
}
if(document.readyState === 'loading'){
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initVideoTracking);
} else {
  initVideoTracking();
}
</script>


<script type="text/javascript">
//Lazyloading Twitter and Insta
function initSocialEmbeds(){
  const options = {threshold: 0.3, rootMargin: "0px 0px 150px 0px"};
  
  const twitter = document.querySelector('.twitter-tweet');
  if(twitter){
    new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
      entries.forEach(entry => {
        if(entry.isIntersecting){
          const script = document.createElement('script');
          script.src = '//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js';
          script.async = true;
          document.head.appendChild(script);
          entry.target.observer?.unobserve(entry.target);
        }
      });
    }, options).observe(twitter);
  }
  
  const instagram = document.querySelector('.instagram-media');
  if(instagram){
    new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
      entries.forEach(entry => {
        if(entry.isIntersecting){
          const script = document.createElement('script');
          script.src = '//www.instagram.com/embed.js';
          script.async = true;
          document.head.appendChild(script);
          entry.target.observer?.unobserve(entry.target);
        }
      });
    }, options).observe(instagram);
  }
}
setTimeout(initSocialEmbeds, 2000);
</script>


<script type="text/javascript">
function initTaboola(){
  const taboolaIds = ['taboola-mid-article-personalisation','taboola-below-article-thumbnails','taboola-below-video-thumbnails','taboola-below-category-thumbnails','taboola-below-photo-thumbnails'];
  const target = taboolaIds.find(id => document.getElementById(id));
  
  if(target){
    new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
      entries.forEach(entry => {
        if(entry.isIntersecting){
          const script = document.createElement('script');
          script.src = '//cdn.taboola.com/libtrc/tv9-hindi/loader.js';
          script.async = true;
          script.onload = () => {
            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({flush: true});
          };
          document.head.appendChild(script);
          entry.target.observer?.unobserve(entry.target);
        }
      });
    }, {rootMargin: '1000px'}).observe(document.getElementById(target));
  }
}
setTimeout(initTaboola, 3000);
</script>


<script>
   function getNewsData(latest_videos_api_url,div_id)
	   {
		   fetch(latest_videos_api_url).then(function (response) 
		   {
				return response.text();
		   }).then(function (html) 
		   {
		   
		   var arrData =  JSON.parse(html);
	       var id, title, url;
		   var strHtml = ''; 
		   //console.log(arrData);
		  
		   var i = 0;
		   arrData.forEach(function(r) 
		   {
				   id = r.id;
				   title  = r.headline.toString();
				   url  = r.url.toString();
				   post_format  = r.post_format.toString();
				   image_url  = r.image_url.toString();
				   
				   if( typeof r.id !== "undefined" ) 
				   {
					    if(i < 10)
						{


strHtml += `<figure class="smallstory by-ajax"> <a href="${url}" title="${title}" data-pos="1" data-widget="Latest Articles" data-cid="${title}">
	  <div class="card_title"><span class="h3">${title}</span></div><div class="imgThumb"> <img width="320" height="180" src="${image_url}" src="https://images.tv9hindi.com/wp-content/themes/tv9bharavarsh/images/watermark-new-small.jpg?ar=16:9" alt="${title}" title="${title}"  class="lazy" loading="lazy" />`;
	  
	  if(post_format == 'video')
	  {
	  	strHtml += `<span class="icon_Comn"><svg><use href="#v_icon"></use></svg></span>`;
	  }
	  strHtml += `</div></a></figure>`;
						
						
						}
						i = i + 1;	
						//console.log(i);
				   }
		   }
		   );
			   //strHtml += '';
			   document.getElementById(div_id).innerHTML = strHtml; // $('#latest_articles_home').html(strHtml); 
		   })
		   .catch(function (err) 
		   {
		   		console.log('Something went wrong.', err);
		   });
		   return false;
   }
	var latest_news_api_url = 'https://www.tv9hindi.com/wp-json/tv9/v1/latest/all';
	var latest_videos_api_url = 'https://www.tv9hindi.com/wp-json/tv9/v1/latest/videos';

	}

<script type="text/javascript">
function initArticleTracking(){
  const dl = window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];

  document.addEventListener('click', e => {
    const link = e.target.closest('a[data-pos]');
    if (!link) return;

    const title = link.getAttribute('title')?.trim() || '';
    const position = link.getAttribute('data-pos')?.trim() || '';
    const widget = link.getAttribute('data-widget')?.trim() || '';
    const cid = link.getAttribute('data-cid')?.trim() || '';

    dl.push({
      event: 'article_click',
      title: title,
      article_position: position,
      widget_name: widget,
      content_id: cid
    });
  }, {passive:true});
}

if(document.readyState === 'loading'){
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initArticleTracking);
} else {
  initArticleTracking();
}
</script>

<script>
var body = document.body;
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  const megaMenuCnt = document.getElementById('megaMenu');
  const hamburger = document.querySelectorAll("#toggleNav, #footMenu");
  const closeBtn = document.querySelector('#closeMenu');

  // Open mega menu
  hamburger.forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
      megaMenuCnt.classList.add('active');
    }, {passive:true});
  });

  // Close mega menu
  closeBtn?.addEventListener("click", () => {
    megaMenuCnt.classList.remove('active');
  }, {passive:true});

  // Submenu toggle with delegation (only ONE listener)
  megaMenuCnt.addEventListener("click", e => {
    const submenu = e.target.closest(".hassubmenu");
    if (!submenu) return;

    const parentUl = submenu.closest("ul");
    const lastActive = parentUl?.querySelector(".hassubmenu.active");

    if (lastActive && lastActive !== submenu) {
      lastActive.classList.remove("active");
    }
    submenu.classList.toggle("active");
  }, {passive:true});
});
